---
title: Riftbound Opus
---
## General

v1.3 of the official Riftbound Core Rules as of March 30th, 2026


## Reference Index

[[#group A|A]] | [[#group B|B]] | [[#group C|C]] | [[#group D|D]] | [[#group E|E]] | [[#group F|F]] | [[#group G|G]] | [[#group H|H]] | [[#group I|I]] | [[#group K|K]] | [[#group L|L]] | [[#group M|M]] | [[#group N|N]] | [[#group O|O]] | [[#group P|P]] | [[#group Q|Q]] | [[#group R|R]] | [[#group S|S]] | [[#group T|T]] | [[#group U|U]] | [[#group V|V]] | [[#group W|W]] | [[#group X|X]] | [[#group Z|Z]]

## Rule Index

## Rules

## rule 000
**000.** Golden and Silver Rules 

### rule 001
**001.** [[#golden rule|Golden Rule ]]

### rule 002
**002.** Card text supersedes rules text. Whenever a card fundamentally contradicts the rules, the card's indication is what is true. 

### rule 050
**050.** [[#silver rule|Silver Rule ]]

### rule 051
**051.** Card text uses different terminology than rules. Card text should be interpreted according to these rules, not as though it were text within these rules. 

### rule 052
**052.** [[#card|Card]], when written in card effects, is shorthand for "[[#main deck|Main Deck ]]card." Runes, legends, and battleﬁelds are not considered cards when executing the abilities and effects of game objects. They are considered cards for the purposes of these rules. 

### rule 053
**053.** Cards refer to themselves in the ﬁrst person. 

#### rule 053.1
**053.1.** * Units and legends say "I," "me," etc. 

#### rule 053.2
**053.2.** * Gear and spells say "this." 

#### rule 053.3
**053.3.** * Battleﬁelds say "here." 

#### rule 053.4
**053.4.** * Cards may refer to themselves by their name for clarity. This is shorthand for the above terms. 

### rule 054
**054.** “Can’t beats Can” 

#### rule 054.1
**054.1.** Cards that forbid actions or effects, as a broad method of determination, supersede cards that allow or permit that same action or effect. 

### rule 055
**055.** When executing card text, do as much as you can, ignoring impossible instructions. 

#### rule 055.1
**055.1.** If all of a card’s instructions are impossible, it is still played and resolved, but nothing happens. 

### rule 056
**056.** Cards a player owns may never be placed into a non-Board zone belonging to another player. 

#### rule 056.1
**056.1.** Non-Board zones corresponding to a player include Main Deck, Rune Deck, Trash, Hand, Chosen Champion zone, and Banishment. 

#### rule 056.2
**056.2.** If a card would enter such a zone, it goes to its owner’s corresponding zone instead. 

## rule 100
**100.** Game Concepts 

### rule 101
**101.** [[#deck construction|Deck Construction ]]

### rule 102
**102.** Riftbound is a Trading Card Game where a player must provide their own cards to play against other players. 

### rule 103
**103.** To play Riftbound, a player must have two [[#decks|Decks, ]]a [[#champion legend|Champion Legend]], and a number of [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]determined by the [[#mode of play|Mode of Play. ]]

#### rule 103.1
**103.1.** 1 [[#champion legend|Champion Legend ]]

#### rule 103.1.a
**103.1.a.** This is placed in the [[#legend zone|Legend Zone ]]at the start of the game. 

#### rule 103.1.b
**103.1.b.** This will dictate the [[#domain identity|Domain Identity ]]of the [[#main deck|Main Deck. ]]

#### rule 103.1.b.1
**103.1.b.1.** Cards included in your [[#decks|Deck ]]must abide by your [[#domain identity|Domain Identity. ]]

#### rule 103.1.b.2
**103.1.b.2.** Your deck’s [[#domain identity|Domain Identity ]]is dictated by the domains of your [[#champion legend|Champion Legend. ]]In the default card frame, these domains appear as symbols in the legend’s upper left corner. 

#### rule 103.1.b.3
**103.1.b.3.** If a card has a single [[#domain|Domain]], then that card is permitted in the [[#domain identity|Domain Identity ]]that corresponds to the same [[#domain|Domain. ]]

#### rule 103.1.b.4
**103.1.b.4.** If a card has more than one [[#domain|Domain]], then that card is permitted only in a [[#domain identity|Domain Identity ]]that contains all of the indicated [[#domain|Domains ]]on that card. 

#### rule 103.2
**103.2.** [[#a main deck of at least 40 cards|A Main Deck of at least 40 cards ]]1 Chosen Champion Unit, Units, Gear, Spells 

#### rule 103.2.a
**103.2.a.** [[#chosen champion|Chosen Champion ]]

#### rule 103.2.a.1
**103.2.a.1.** This will be placed in the [[#champion zone|Champion Zone ]]at the start of the game. 

#### rule 103.2.a.2
**103.2.a.2.** Must be a champion unit with a champion tag that matches the tag on your [[#champion legend|Champion Legend. ]]Example: Loose Cannon has the tag Jinx. Therefore, a player could choose Jinx, Rebel or Jinx, Demolitionist as their [[#chosen champion|Chosen Champion]], because they also have the tag Jinx. Example: Tibbers has the tag Annie, but it is a signature unit, not a champion unit. It cannot be your [[#chosen champion|Chosen Champion]], even if your [[#champion legend|Champion Legend ]]has the tag Annie. 

#### rule 103.2.a.3
**103.2.a.3.** A player’s [[#chosen champion|Chosen Champion ]]is both the speciﬁc card chosen for this slot during Deck Building and also any [[#champion unit|Champion Unit ]]with the same name as the speciﬁc card selected for this speciﬁc slot during the course of play.  Example: A player chose Jinx, Rebel as their Chosen Champion. One copy of Jinx, Rebel starts the game in their Chosen Champion zone. Any additional copies of Jinx, Rebel in their Main Deck, their hand, their trash, or on the board also count as their Chosen Champion for any game rules and effects that care about Chosen Champion status during the game. 

#### rule 103.2.b
**103.2.b.** Your [[#main deck|Main Deck ]]can include up to 3 copies of the same named card. 

#### rule 103.2.b.1
**103.2.b.1.** This includes your [[#chosen champion|Chosen Champion. ]]Example: A deck could include Volibear, Furious as its [[#chosen champion|Chosen Champion ]]and still include 2 more copies of Volibear, Furious. 

#### rule 103.2.b.2
**103.2.b.2.** Cards have different names even if they represent the same character. Example: A deck could include 3 copies of Yasuo, Remorseful and 3 copies of Yasuo, Windrider, because they have different names. 

#### rule 103.2.c
**103.2.c.** Subject to [[#domain identity|Domain Identity. ]]

#### rule 103.2.d
**103.2.d.** Your deck may only contain 3 total [[#signature|Signature ]]cards that have the same Champion tag as your [[#champion legend|Champion Legend. ]]

#### rule 103.2.d.1
**103.2.d.1.** Regardless of name, a deck may only contain a sum total of 3 Signature cards. 

#### rule 103.2.d.2
**103.2.d.2.** All of the Signature cards must have the Champion tag that corresponds to the [[#champion legend|Champion Legend ]]of the deck. 

#### rule 103.2.d.3
**103.2.d.3.** Signature cards are not Champion units and cannot be placed in the [[#champion zone|Champion Zone]]. 

#### rule 103.2.e
**103.2.e.** During Gameplay, the [[#main deck|Main Deck ]]is [[#secret information|Secret Information. ]]

#### rule 103.2.e.1
**103.2.e.1.** It cannot be looked through or revealed unless instructed by a card effect. 

#### rule 103.3
**103.3.** [[#rune deck|Rune Deck ]]

#### rule 103.3.a
**103.3.a.** 12 [[#rune|Rune Cards ]]

#### rule 103.3.a.1
**103.3.a.1.** Cards in this deck must be of the [[#domain identity|Domain Identity ]]of your [[#champion legend|Champion Legend. ]]

#### rule 103.3.b
**103.3.b.** Must be shuffled and kept separate from the [[#main deck|Main Deck. ]]

#### rule 103.4
**103.4.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]

#### rule 103.4.a
**103.4.a.** The number will be dictated by your [[#mode of play|Mode of Play. ]]

#### rule 103.4.b
**103.4.b.** Subject to [[#domain identity|Domain Identity ]]if applicable. 

#### rule 103.4.c
**103.4.c.** Cannot include more than one of a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]of the same name when there are more than one required for the deck. 

### rule 104
**104.** [[#setup|Setup ]]

### rule 105
**105.** Spaces 

### rule 106
**106.** The [[#play area|Play Area ]]is a collection of logical [[##zones|Zones ]]that are deﬁned by their behaviors and relationships to [[##player|Players. ]]These [[#zones|Zones ]]are grouped into [[#board|The Board ]]and [[#non-board zones|Non-Board Zones. ]]

### rule 107
**107.** [[#board|The Board ]]

#### rule 107.1
**107.1.** [[#bases|Bases ]]

#### rule 107.1.a
**107.1.a.** Each player has their own [[#bases|Base. ]]

#### rule 107.1.b
**107.1.b.** Each Base is a [[#location|Location. ]]

#### rule 107.1.c
**107.1.c.** [[#permanents|Permanents ]]and [[#rune|Runes ]]controlled by a player reside in that player's [[#bases|Base. ]]

#### rule 107.1.c.1
**107.1.c.1.** [[#permanents|Permanents ]]attached to [[#permanents|Permanents ]]controlled by a player may also be found in that player’s [[#bases|Base. ]]

#### rule 107.1.d
**107.1.d.** [[#permanents|Permanents ]]and [[#rune|Runes ]]in [[#bases|Bases ]]are [[#public information|Public Information. ]]

#### rule 107.2
**107.2.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld Zone ]]

#### rule 107.2.a
**107.2.a.** The [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld Zone ]]houses multiple [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds. ]]

#### rule 107.2.b
**107.2.b.** Each [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]is individually a [[#location|Location. ]]

#### rule 107.2.c
**107.2.c.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]and permanents at [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]are [[#public information|Public Information. ]]

#### rule 107.3
**107.3.** [[#facedown zones|Facedown Zones ]]

#### rule 107.3.a
**107.3.a.** Each Battleﬁeld is associated with a sub-zone called a [[#facedown zones|Facedown Zone]], a single logical space that a card can be put facedown in through various [[#game effects|Game Effects. ]]

#### rule 107.3.b
**107.3.b.** Each [[#facedown zones|Facedown Zone ]]has a maximum occupancy of one card. 

#### rule 107.3.b.1
**107.3.b.1.** The maximum occupancy of a [[#facedown zones|Facedown Zone ]]can increase or decrease. 

#### rule 107.3.b.2
**107.3.b.2.** If the maximum occupancy of a [[#facedown zones|Facedown Zone ]]decreases to a number less than the number of cards currently located there, the controller of that [[#facedown zones|Facedown Zone ]]must put a number of cards equal to the difference in the trash from the [[#facedown zones|Facedown Zone. ]]

#### rule 107.3.c
**107.3.c.** Cards can only be placed in or occupy the [[#facedown zones|Facedown Zone ]]if the controller of the card also controls the associated [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld. ]]

#### rule 107.3.d
**107.3.d.** If a player loses [[#control|Control ]]of a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld]], any cards in the [[#facedown zones|Facedown Zone ]]associated with that [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]are removed during the next [[#cleanup|Cleanup. ]]See [[##rule 318|rule 318.]] [[#cleanup|Cleanups]] for more information. See [[##rule 421|rule 421.]] [[#hide|Hide]] for more information. 

#### rule 107.3.e
**107.3.e.** Facedown Zones are not locations. 

#### rule 107.4
**107.4.** [[#legend zone|Legend Zone ]]

#### rule 107.4.a
**107.4.a.** The space for each player's [[#champion legend|Champion Legend. ]]

#### rule 107.4.b
**107.4.b.** This is not a location. 

#### rule 107.4.c
**107.4.c.** The [[#champion legend|Champion Legend ]]here is a [[#game object|Game Object. ]]See [[##rule 120|rule 120.]] [[#game object|Game Objects]] for more information. 

#### rule 107.4.d
**107.4.d.** The [[#champion legend|Champion Legend ]]cannot be removed, moved, or displaced from this zone. 

### rule 108
**108.** [[#non-board zones|Non-Board Zones. ]]

#### rule 108.1
**108.1.** [[#chain|The Chain ]]

#### rule 108.1.a
**108.1.a.** Cards and abilities are placed here as part of the process of being [[#played|played. ]]See [[##rule 327|rule 327.]] [[#chain|Chains]] for more information. 

#### rule 108.1.b
**108.1.b.** Cards and abilities on the [[#chain|Chain ]]are [[#public information|Public Information. ]]

#### rule 108.2
**108.2.** [[#trashes|Trashes ]]

#### rule 108.2.a
**108.2.a.** Each player has their own [[#trashes|Trash. ]]

#### rule 108.2.b
**108.2.b.** This space is where cards are placed when they are killed or discarded, when they ﬁnish being executed as spells, when they are moved to the trash as an effect, etc. 

#### rule 108.2.c
**108.2.c.** Cards in each player’s [[#trashes|Trash ]]are [[#unordered|unordered. ]]Their sequence does not matter, and they may be reorganized. 

#### rule 108.2.d
**108.2.d.** Cards in a player's [[#trashes|Trash ]]are Public [[#information|Information. ]]See [[##rule 128|rule 128.]] [[#privacy|Privacy]] for more information. 

#### rule 108.3
**108.3.** [[#champion zone|Champion Zones ]]

#### rule 108.3.a
**108.3.a.** Each player has their own [[#champion zone|Champion Zone. ]]

#### rule 108.3.b
**108.3.b.** The space each player puts their [[#chosen champion|Chosen Champion ]]at the start of the game. 

#### rule 108.3.c
**108.3.c.** The [[#chosen champion|Chosen Champion ]]cannot be returned to this zone by normal means. 

#### rule 108.3.c.1
**108.3.c.1.** If a [[#chosen champion|Chosen Champion ]]is instructed to be returned to this zone, it can only do so if there is not a card already in this zone. 

#### rule 108.3.d
**108.3.d.** The [[#chosen champion|Chosen Champion ]]can be played from here as normal, following the rules of [[#playing a card|Playing a Card.  ]]See [[##rule 349|rule 349.]] [[#playing cards|Playing Cards]] for more information. 

#### rule 108.3.e
**108.3.e.** Cards in a player’s [[#champion zone|Champion Zone ]]are [[#public information|Public Information. ]]

#### rule 108.4
**108.4.** [[#main deck|Main Deck Zones ]]

#### rule 108.4.a
**108.4.a.** Each player has their own [[#main deck|Main Deck Zone. ]]

#### rule 108.4.b
**108.4.b.** The space for the player's [[#main deck|Main Deck. ]]

#### rule 108.4.c
**108.4.c.** Primarily houses the face-down deck during gameplay. 

#### rule 108.4.d
**108.4.d.** The order of cards in the deck is [[#secret information|Secret Information ]]during the course of play.  See [[##rule 128|rule 128.]] [[#privacy|Privacy]] for more information. 

#### rule 108.5
**108.5.** [[#rune deck|Rune Deck Zones ]]

#### rule 108.5.a
**108.5.a.** Each player has their own [[#rune deck|Rune Deck Zone. ]]

#### rule 108.5.b
**108.5.b.** The space for the player's [[#rune deck|Rune Deck. ]]

#### rule 108.5.c
**108.5.c.** Primarily houses the face-down runes during gameplay. 

#### rule 108.5.d
**108.5.d.** The order of runes in the deck is [[#secret information|Secret Information ]]during the course of play.  See [[##rule 128|rule 128.]] [[#privacy|Privacy]] for more information. 

#### rule 108.6
**108.6.** [[#banishments|Banishments ]]

#### rule 108.6.a
**108.6.a.** Each player has their own [[#banishments|Banishment. ]]

#### rule 108.6.b
**108.6.b.** This space is where cards are placed when they are banished by a spell or effect. 

#### rule 108.6.c
**108.6.c.** Represents cards that have been removed from play in a more difﬁcult-to-recover way, or a temporary space to hold cards while effects are being processed. 

#### rule 108.6.d
**108.6.d.** The cards in the banishment are [[#unordered|unordered. ]]Their sequence does not matter, and they may be reorganized. 

#### rule 108.6.e
**108.6.e.** The cards in any player's [[#banishments|Banishment ]]are Public [[#information|Information. ]]See [[##rule 128|rule 128.]] [[#privacy|Privacy]] for more information. 

#### rule 108.7
**108.7.** [[#hand|The Hand ]]

#### rule 108.7.a
**108.7.a.** Each player has their own [[#hand|Hand. ]]

#### rule 108.7.b
**108.7.b.** This is the location cards go when [[#drawn|Drawn. ]]

#### rule 108.7.c
**108.7.c.** The cards in a player's hand are [[#private information|Private Information. ]]

#### rule 108.7.d
**108.7.d.** The number of cards in a player's hand is [[#public information|Public Information. ]]

#### rule 108.7.e
**108.7.e.** The hand can be targeted as a zone, and cards there can be affected by spells and effects when speciﬁed. 

### rule 109
**109.** All [[#game object|Game Objects ]]in the collective [[#play area|Play Areas ]]are [[#public information|Public Information. ]]

#### rule 109.1
**109.1.** Any player may view, or be provided with the details of the face-up information printed on the cards in the [[#play area|Play Area. ]]

#### rule 109.2
**109.2.** The [[#state|State ]]of all [[#game object|Game Objects ]]in the [[#play area|Play Area ]]is also [[#public information|Public Information.  ]]Examples:   If a [[#unit|Unit ]]is [[#buffed|Buffed  ]]If a [[#gear|Gear ]]is [[#exhausted|Exhausted  ]]Etc. 

### rule 110
**110.** Whenever a [[#game object|Game Object ]]changes zones to or from a [[#non-board zones|Non-Board Zone]], all [[#temporary modiﬁcations|Temporary Modiﬁcations ]]of all kinds cease to be tracked on it in all capacities.  Examples:  Damage is cleared.  [[#buffed|Buffs ]]are removed.  Granted [[#keywords|Keywords ]]are no longer granted. 

### rule 111
**111.** Setup Process 

### rule 112
**112.** Each player separates their [[#champion legend|Champion Legend ]]and places it in the [[#legend zone|Legend Zone. ]]

### rule 113
**113.** Each player separates their [[#chosen champion|Chosen Champion ]]and places it in the [[#champion zone|Champion Zone. ]]

### rule 114
**114.** Each player sets aside their [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds. ]]

#### rule 114.1
**114.1.** Your [[#mode of play|Mode of Play ]]will dictate how these are used and placed into the [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld Zone.  ]]See [[##rule 476|rule 476.]] [[#modes of play|Modes of Play]] for more information. 

### rule 115
**115.** Each player shuffles their decks, separately, then places them into their respective Zones. 

#### rule 115.1
**115.1.** The [[#main deck|Main Deck ]]is placed in the [[#main deck|Main Deck Zone. ]]

#### rule 115.2
**115.2.** The [[#rune deck|Rune Deck ]]is placed in the [[#rune deck|Rune Deck Zone. ]]

### rule 116
**116.** Determine [[#turn order|Turn Order ]]using any fair random method agreed on by all players. 

#### rule 116.1
**116.1.** [[#turn order|Turn Order ]]is established as a repeating set of the players. 

#### rule 116.1.a
**116.1.a.** The [[#mode of play|Mode of Play ]]will specify how to determine a [[#first player|First Player. ]]

#### rule 116.1.b
**116.1.b.** If not otherwise speciﬁed, [[#seating|Seating ]]then determines the sequence, play proceeding clockwise from the [[#first player|First Player. ]]

#### rule 116.1.b.1
**116.1.b.1.** The [[#first player|First Player ]]is the player who becomes the [[#turn player|Turn Player ]]ﬁrst. 

#### rule 116.1.c
**116.1.c.** The [[#turn order|Turn Order ]]generates a looping queue of turns, starting with the First Player and repeating until the game ends. 

#### rule 116.2
**116.2.** See the selected [[#mode of play|Mode of Play ]]for any adjustments to each player's ﬁrst turn.  See [[##rule 476|rule 476.]] [[#modes of play|Modes of Play]] for more information. 

### rule 117
**117.** Players each draw 4. 

### rule 118
**118.** In turn order, players perform their [[#mulligan|Mulligan. ]]

#### rule 118.1
**118.1.** A player may choose up to two cards in their hand. They set those cards aside. 

#### rule 118.2
**118.2.** Then, that player draws as many cards as they set aside. 

#### rule 118.3
**118.3.** Finally, that player [[#recycles|Recycles ]]the cards that were set aside.  See [[##rule 416|rule 416.]] [[#recycles|Recycle]] for more information. 

### rule 119
**119.** Begin play with the [[#first player|First Player ]]taking their turn. 

### rule 120
**120.** [[#game object|Game Objects ]]

### rule 121
**121.** A [[#game object|Game Object ]]is any game piece that can produce one or more [[#game effects|Game Effects ]]or grant prerequisites for players to take [[#game actions|Game Actions. ]]

### rule 122
**122.** A [[#game object|Game Object ]]does not include nor preclude any inherent properties beyond the ability to produce, or act as the prerequisite for, [[#game effects|Game Effects ]]and [[#game actions|Game Actions. ]]

### rule 123
**123.** A [[#game object|Game Object ]]can be a literal object or a logical object. 

### rule 124
**124.** [[#game object|Game Objects ]]include, but are not limited to, the following:  Main Deck cards in any zone  Runes in any zone  Legends  Battleﬁelds  Tokens in any zone Abilities of any type on the chain  Buffs and other status markers 

### rule 125
**125.** [[#card|Cards ]]

### rule 126
**126.** Riftbound games are composed of players playing the cards in their respective decks. 

### rule 127
**127.** [[#ownership|Ownership ]]

#### rule 127.1
**127.1.** For gameplay purposes, a card's [[#ownership|Owner ]]is the player who brought it into the game, either as their [[#champion legend|Champion Legend]], one of their [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds]], or part of their [[#main deck|Main Deck ]]or [[#rune deck|Rune Deck]]. The legal owner of a card doesn't matter during gameplay.  Example: Bo didn't bring a deck, so Alice loans him a deck. During the game, Bo is considered the owner of those cards, even though legally they belong to Alice. 

### rule 128
**128.** [[#privacy|Privacy ]]

#### rule 128.1
**128.1.** A card will always exist in one of the many [[#zones|Zones ]]described during [[#setup|Setup. ]]

#### rule 128.2
**128.2.** A card will have a different level of [[#privacy|Privacy ]]based on where it resides at a given time 

#### rule 128.3
**128.3.** [[#secret|Secret: ]]This level of Privacy indicates that no player may read or look at the face of the card. 

#### rule 128.4
**128.4.** [[#private|Private: ]]This level of Privacy indicates that only the controller of a card on the board or the owner of a card in any other zone may read or look at the face of the card.  Example: Cards in a player's hand are owned by that player. Only that player may read or look at their faces.  Example: If a player controls a facedown card at a battleﬁeld, that player and only that player may read or look at that card's face, regardless of who owns that card. 

#### rule 128.5
**128.5.** [[#public|Public: ]]This level of Privacy indicates that any player may read or look at the face of the card. 

### rule 129
**129.** [[#back side|Back Side ]]

#### rule 129.1
**129.1.** The back side of a card is the side with the [[#riftbound|Riftbound ]]logo. 

#### rule 129.2
**129.2.** There is a unique pattern of back side for each of the three categories of card: [[#main deck|Main Deck ]]cards, [[#rune deck|Rune Deck ]]cards, and [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]and [[#champion legend|Champion Legends. ]]

#### rule 129.3
**129.3.** The back side of a card is presented to conceal information for [[#private|Private ]]and [[#secret|Secret ]]information cards. For example, cards in the [[#main deck|Main Deck ]]and cards in hand have their back side presented. 

#### rule 129.4
**129.4.** The term [[#facedown zones|facedown ]]is used to describe the state during regular play of having a card's back side presented on the Board. A facedown card’s front side is considered [[#private information|Private Information. ]]

### rule 130
**130.** [[#front side|Front Side ]]

#### rule 130.1
**130.1.** The front side of a card is the opposite of its back. 

#### rule 130.2
**130.2.** This is also referred to as a [[#front face|front face. ]]

#### rule 130.3
**130.3.** This can be identiﬁed in situations where the back is not easily discernible by the presence of the [[#play cost|Play Cost ]]in the upper left corner of the card. 

#### rule 130.4
**130.4.** Cards, when played, are played with their front face presented. 

#### rule 130.5
**130.5.** The term [[#face up|face up ]]is used to describe the state during regular play of having a card's front face presented 

#### rule 130.6
**130.6.** Cards are considered to be [[#public information|Public Information ]]while in this state, even if obscured by other cards in a pile. Example: The Trash is [[#public information|Public Information ]]because all cards there have their front face presented even while stacked. 

### rule 131
**131.** [[#cost|Cost ]]

#### rule 131.1
**131.1.** [[#main deck|Main Deck ]]cards have a [[#cost|Cost]], listed in the upper left corner of the front face of the card. See [[##rule 164|rule 164.]] [[#rune pool|Rune Pools]] for more information. 

#### rule 131.2
**131.2.** [[#energy|Energy ]]Cost 

#### rule 131.2.a
**131.2.a.** The numeral listed in the [[#cost|Cost ]]element in the upper left corner of the card. 

#### rule 131.3
**131.3.** [[#power|Power ]]cost 

#### rule 131.3.a
**131.3.a.** The symbols, listed vertically, in the [[#cost|Cost ]]element in the upper left corner of the card. 

#### rule 131.3.b
**131.3.b.** This section may not be present on every card. 

#### rule 131.4
**131.4.** Effects that need to determine a card’s cost for any purpose always use its printed cost, even if that cost is altered or ignored as the card is played.  Example: Sky Splitter is a spell that costs 8 Energy and says in part “This spell's Energy cost is reduced by the highest Might among units you control.” Lux, Illuminated is a unit that says “When you play a spell that costs 5 or more, give me +3 [M] this turn.” If a player who controls Lux plays Sky Splitter, Lux’s ability will trigger, regardless of how much was actually paid for Sky Splitter. 

### rule 132
**132.** [[#name|Name ]]

#### rule 132.1
**132.1.** Each card has a name that identiﬁes it uniquely. 

#### rule 132.2
**132.2.** This is usually located in the middle of the card. 

#### rule 132.3
**132.3.** Cards that are printed in different languages but represent the same card are considered to have the same name for the purposes of deckbuilding and gameplay.  Example: Chemtech Enforcer in English and its counterpart in Chinese are considered the same card, despite the [[#name|Name ]]element on the card reading differently. 

#### rule 132.4
**132.4.** Some cards have both a short name and a subtitle. For all purposes, including rules and deckbuilding, such a card’s name is “[Short Name], [Subtitle]”. Example: Kai’Sa, Evolutionary and Kai’Sa, Survivor both have the short name Kai’Sa, but they have different names. You can include 3 of each in your deck under normal deckbuilding rules. If one of them is your Chosen Champion, the other is not. 

### rule 133
**133.** [[#category|Category ]]

#### rule 133.1
**133.1.** A card can have one or more [[#category|Categories ]]and [[#sub-categories|Sub-Categories ]]based on the properties of its front and back sides. 

#### rule 133.2
**133.2.** These [[#category|Categories ]]and [[#sub-categories|Sub-Categories ]]dictate the behaviors of the card during play. 

#### rule 133.3
**133.3.** Spells and other effects can refer to categories, sub-categories, supertypes, card types, tags, and other characteristics inclusively or exclusively.  Example: A "non-unit card" is any card that is not a unit.  Example: A "unit" is any game object that is a unit, regardless of any other categories it belongs to. 

#### rule 133.4
**133.4.** [[#main deck|Main Deck Cards ]]begin the game in the [[#main deck|Main Deck ]]or (in the case of a [[#chosen champion|Chosen Champion]]) the [[#champion zone|Champion Zone. ]]

#### rule 133.4.a
**133.4.a.** [[#permanents|Permanents ]]

#### rule 133.4.a.1
**133.4.a.1.** An umbrella sub-category encompassing [[#main deck|Main Deck ]]Game Objects that remain on the board after being played. 

#### rule 133.4.a.2
**133.4.a.2.** [[#unit|Unit ]]and [[#gear|Gear ]]are permanent types. 

#### rule 133.4.b
**133.4.b.** [[#spells|Spells ]]

#### rule 133.4.b.1
**133.4.b.1.** A sub-category encompassing Main Deck cards with the spell type, which do not remain on the board after being played. 

#### rule 133.5
**133.5.** [[#rune deck|Rune Deck Cards ]]begin the game in the [[#rune deck|Rune Deck. ]]

#### rule 133.5.a
**133.5.a.** [[#rune|Runes ]]

#### rule 133.5.a.1
**133.5.a.1.** A sub-category encompassing cards with the rune type. These are [[#channeled|channeled ]]rather than played. They remain on the board after being channeled, but they are not permanents, as they are not [[#main deck|Main Deck ]]cards. 

#### rule 133.6
**133.6.** [[#non-deck cards|Non-Deck Cards ]]are not part of any deck and begin the game in a zone determined by their type. 

#### rule 133.6.a
**133.6.a.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]

#### rule 133.6.a.1
**133.6.a.1.** A sub-category encompassing cards with the battleﬁeld type. They are not played or channeled. They start the game on the board. 

#### rule 133.6.b
**133.6.b.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]

#### rule 133.6.b.1
**133.6.b.1.** A sub-category encompassing cards with the legend type. They are not played or channeled. They start the game in the Legend Zone and cannot leave it during play. 

#### rule 133.7
**133.7.** [[#supertypes|Supertypes ]]are [[#category|Categories ]]that may apply to game objects of multiple types. They are listed before a card’s type. 

#### rule 133.7.a
**133.7.a.** [[#champion zone|Champion ]]is a supertype that applies exclusively to units. It impacts the rules for deckbuilding. See [[##rule 103.2.a|rule 103.2.a.]] [[#chosen champion|Chosen Champion]] for more information. 

#### rule 133.7.b
**133.7.b.** [[#signature|Signature ]]is a supertype that may apply to game objects of any card type. It impacts the rules for deckbuilding. See [[##rule 103.2.d|rule 103.2.d.]]for more information about [[#signature|Signature cards. ]]

#### rule 133.7.c
**133.7.c.** [[#token|Token ]]is a supertype applied to temporary game objects of any card type. See [[##rule 176|rule 176.]] [[#token|Tokens]] for more information. 

#### rule 133.8
**133.8.** [[#tags|Tags ]]are [[#category|Categories ]]that may apply to game objects of multiple types. They are listed after a card’s type. 

#### rule 133.8.a
**133.8.a.** [[#tags|Tags ]]have no innate rules meaning, but may be referenced by game rules and card effects. 

#### rule 133.8.b
**133.8.b.** [[#tags|Tags ]]used to link [[#legend zone|Legends]], [[#champion unit|Champion Units]], and [[#signature|Signature ]]cards are known as [[#champion tags|Champion Tags. ]]

### rule 134
**134.** [[#domain|Domain ]]

#### rule 134.1
**134.1.** Most cards belong to one or more of six [[#domain|Domains]], identiﬁed by one or more symbols in the lower right corner. 

#### rule 134.2
**134.2.** Each Domain has an associated color, a unique symbol, and a shorthand used to represent that symbol in written text. 

#### rule 134.2.a
**134.2.a.** [[#fury|Fury ]]is associated with the color red and represented by a circular symbol with three projecting points. Its shorthand is [R]. 

#### rule 134.2.b
**134.2.b.** [[#calm|Calm ]]is associated with the color green and represented by a symbol resembling a leaf. Its shorthand is [G]. 

#### rule 134.2.c
**134.2.c.** [[#mind|Mind ]]is associated with the color blue and represented by a symbol resembling a sun and moon. Its shorthand is [B]. 

#### rule 134.2.d
**134.2.d.** [[#board|Body ]]is associated with the color orange and represented by a blocky diamond-shaped symbol. Its shorthand is [O]. 

#### rule 134.2.e
**134.2.e.** [[#chaos|Chaos ]]is associated with the color purple and represented by a hexagonal symbol with swirls emanating from its center. Its shorthand is [P]. 

#### rule 134.2.f
**134.2.f.** [[#order|Order ]]is associated with the color yellow and represented by an angular winged symbol. Its shorthand is [Y]. 

### rule 135
**135.** [[#rules text|Rules Text ]]

#### rule 135.1
**135.1.** All cards have a section that describes how they affect the game. This section is known as the [[#rules text|Rules Text ]]of the card. 

#### rule 135.2
**135.2.** This section may contain: 

#### rule 135.2.a
**135.2.a.** [[#abilities|Abilities ]]

#### rule 135.2.a.1
**135.2.a.1.** Abilities are discrete pieces of text that describe what a card may or must do.  See [[##rule 360|rule 360.]] [[#abilities|Abilities]] for more information. 

#### rule 135.2.a.2
**135.2.a.2.** They may appear on any card. 

#### rule 135.2.b
**135.2.b.** [[#instructions|Instructions ]]

#### rule 135.2.b.1
**135.2.b.1.** Instructions are a type of text that appears on spells and within abilities. 

#### rule 135.2.b.2
**135.2.b.2.** They describe the actions to be taken as the spell or ability resolves. 

#### rule 135.2.b.3
**135.2.b.3.** Instructions will self-describe when they are to be executed. If there is no timing described, they will execute during resolution. Example: An instruction says “as you play me, kill a unit as an additional cost.” That instruction will execute as the card is being played. If the card is given Repeat and the Repeat cost is paid, this instruction will not execute because the Repeat execution does not happen until resolution of the spell, after this instruction has executed.  

#### rule 135.2.b.4
**135.2.b.4.** Instructions can usually be recognized by the way they are written. An instruction is written in the imperative mood, using the base form of a verb and omitting the subject unless necessary. 

#### rule 135.2.c
**135.2.c.** [[#keywords|Keywords ]]

#### rule 135.2.c.1
**135.2.c.1.** Keywords are short words or phrases that represent longer abilities or instructions. See [[##rule 800|rule 800.]] [[#keywords|Keywords]] for more information. 

#### rule 135.2.c.2
**135.2.c.2.** Keywords may or may not have reminder text. 

#### rule 135.2.d
**135.2.d.** [[#reminder text|Reminder Text ]]

#### rule 135.2.d.1
**135.2.d.1.** Reminder text appears in italics and parentheses. 

#### rule 135.2.d.2
**135.2.d.2.** Its purpose is to summarize relevant rules, including keywords and other rules. 

#### rule 135.2.d.3
**135.2.d.3.** The presence, absence, or exact wording of reminder text has no effect on game function. 

#### rule 135.2.e
**135.2.e.** [[#symbols|Symbols ]]

#### rule 135.2.e.1
**135.2.e.1.** Rules text sometimes contains symbols that express game concepts. Each symbol also has a shorthand used to represent it in written text. 

#### rule 135.2.e.2
**135.2.e.2.** The cost of [[#exhausted|Exhausting ]]a [[#permanents|Permanent ]]is represented by the “exhaust symbol,” which resembles a card turning sideways. Its shorthand is [E]. (Some previous rules information has given its shorthand as [T].) 

#### rule 135.2.e.3
**135.2.e.3.** [[#might|Might ]]is represented by the “Might symbol,” which resembles a sword and shield. Its shorthand is [M]. (Some previous rules information has given its shorthand as [S].) 

#### rule 135.2.e.4
**135.2.e.4.** [[#power|Power ]]of a speciﬁc [[#domain|Domain ]]is represented by its domain symbol and the corresponding shorthand. See [[##rule 134|rule 134.]] [[#domain|Domain]] for more information. 

#### rule 135.2.e.5
**135.2.e.5.** Power of any [[#domain|Domain ]]is represented by a swirling rainbow symbol. Its shorthand is [A]. 

#### rule 135.2.e.5.a
**135.2.e.5.a.** When required as a cost, [A] can be paid by [[#power|Power ]]of any [[#domain|Domain]]. 

#### rule 135.2.e.5.b
**135.2.e.5.b.** When [[#added|Added ]]to a player’s [[#rune pool|Rune Pool, ]][A] can be spent to pay a [[#power|Power ]]cost of any [[#domain|Domain. ]]

#### rule 135.2.e.6
**135.2.e.6.** Power of a domain corresponding to a card’s own [[#domain|Domain ]]is not represented by a symbol, but appears in these rules similarly to other symbols. Its shorthand is [C]. 

#### rule 135.2.e.6.a
**135.2.e.6.a.** When a [C] shorthand is printed on a card as reminder text, it assumes that card’s usual [[#domain|Domain]], but it still means “one Power of this card’s [[#domain|Domain]].” 

#### rule 135.2.e.6.b
**135.2.e.6.b.** A [C] shorthand on a card with no [[#domain|Domain ]]or with multiple [[#domain|Domains ]]is processed as [A] instead. 

#### rule 135.2.e.7
**135.2.e.7.** A keyword associated with an ability is indicated by the [>] symbol. 

#### rule 135.2.e.7.a
**135.2.e.7.a.** This could be a dependent keyword like [Legion][>] or [Level][>], or it could be a permissive keyword like [Action][>] or [Reaction][>]. 

#### rule 135.2.e.7.b
**135.2.e.7.b.** Whatever instruction or ability comes after the [>] is modiﬁed by the keyword that comes before the [>]. Either it will be inactive, in the case of a dependent keyword, or it will receive the permission granted by the keyword in the case of a permissive keyword. 

#### rule 135.3
**135.3.** Rules text can be blank. 

#### rule 135.4
**135.4.** A card’s printed [[#rules text|Rules Text ]]is [[#inactive|Inactive ]]while that card is [[#attached|Attached ]]to another card. See [[##rule 716|rule 716.]] [[#attachment|Attachment]] for more information. See [[##rule 720|rule 720.]] [[#inactive|Inactive]] for more information. 

#### rule 135.4.a
**135.4.a.** The presence of text, rules, [[#keywords|Keywords]], and other effects can still be referenced and detected by other game effects, even while [[#rules text|Rules Text ]]is [[#inactive|Inactive. ]]

#### rule 135.4.b
**135.4.b.** Any granted or appended [[#rules text|Rules Text ]]on a card is still [[#active|Active ]]even if that card is [[#attached|Attached ]]to another card. 

### rule 136
**136.** [[#effect text|Effect Text ]]

#### rule 136.1
**136.1.** Some cards have a separate section of text below the [[#rules text|Rules Text]]. This is referred to as the [[#effect text|Effect Text]].  

#### rule 136.2
**136.2.** [[#effect text|Effect Text ]]can contain additional [[#abilities|Abilities. ]]

#### rule 136.2.a
**136.2.a.** [[#effect text|Effect Text ]]can be blank. 

#### rule 136.2.b
**136.2.b.** [[#effect text|Effect Text ]]is [[#inactive|inactive ]]unless the card with the [[#effect text|Effect Text ]]is [[#attached|Attached ]]to another card. See [[##rule 716|rule 716.]] [[#attachment|Attachment]] for more information. See [[##rule 720|rule 720.]] [[#inactive|Inactive]] for more information. 

#### rule 136.2.c
**136.2.c.** The abilities in the [[#effect text|Effect Text ]]section of a card are appended to the [[#rules text|Rules Text ]]of the card to which the card with the [[#effect text|Effect Text ]]is [[#attached|Attached. ]]

### rule 137
**137.** [[#might bonus|Might Bonus ]]

#### rule 137.1
**137.1.** Some cards have a [[#might bonus|Might Bonus ]]in their lower right corner, expressed as an operator plus an integer. 

#### rule 137.2
**137.2.** A card’s [[#might bonus|Might Bonus ]]can be +0. 

#### rule 137.3
**137.3.** A card’s [[#might bonus|Might Bonus ]]modulates the [[#might|Might ]]of the card to which the card that has the [[#might bonus|Might Bonus ]]is [[#attached|Attached]]. See [[##rule 716|rule 716.]] [[#attachment|Attachment]] for more information. 

#### rule 137.3.a
**137.3.a.** The [[#might bonus|Might Bonus ]]is applied while [[#attached|Attached ]]and stops applying as soon as the card with the [[#might bonus|Might Bonus ]]is no longer [[#attached|Attached. ]]

#### rule 137.3.b
**137.3.b.** If the card to which a card with a [[#might bonus|Might Bonus ]]is [[#attached|Attached ]]has no [[#might|Might ]]value, the [[#might bonus|Might Bonus ]]is ignored. 

### rule 138
**138.** [[#flavor text|Flavor Text ]]

#### rule 138.1
**138.1.** Flavor text is text that appears at the bottom of some cards to provide aesthetic enjoyment. It conveys no gameplay information.  Example: The card Void Seeker features a quote from the character Kai'Sa. It does not have the Kai'Sa tag and has no gameplay connection to the Champion unit Kai'Sa. 

#### rule 138.2
**138.2.** Flavor text is located at the bottom of the section provided for rules text, usually in a shaded bar. It appears in italics. 

### rule 139
**139.** [[#illustration|Illustration ]]

#### rule 139.1
**139.1.** Each card has an illustration. It conveys no gameplay information. 

### rule 140
**140.** [[#unit|Units ]]

### rule 141
**141.** [[#unit|Unit is]]: 

#### rule 141.1
**141.1.** A [[#game object|Game Object ]]

#### rule 141.1.a
**141.1.a.** While on [[#board|the Board]]: 

#### rule 141.1.a.1
**141.1.a.1.** [[#unit|Units ]]are at one of several [[#location|Locations ]]while on [[#board|the Board]]: a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]or their [[#bases|Base. ]]

#### rule 141.1.a.2
**141.1.a.2.** [[#unit|Units ]]and their details are Public Information while on [[#board|the Board. ]]

#### rule 141.1.a.3
**141.1.a.3.** [[#unit|Units ]]can be chosen, affected, or manipulated by spells, affects, or game actions that specify [[#unit|Units. ]]

#### rule 141.1.a.4
**141.1.a.4.** [[#unit|Units ]]can be [[#killed|Killed.  ]]See [[##rule 428|rule 428.]] [[#killed|Kill]] for more information. 

#### rule 141.1.b
**141.1.b.** While in the [[#trashes|Trash: ]]

#### rule 141.1.b.1
**141.1.b.1.** [[#unit|Units ]]are treated as [[#card|Cards]], similar to when in the [[#hand|Hand. ]]

#### rule 141.1.b.2
**141.1.b.2.** They retain the properties of being a [[#unit|Unit]], but are not on [[#board|the Board ]]and thus cannot take actions or be affected by spells, abilities, or game actions that target [[#unit|Units ]]on [[#board|the Board. ]]

#### rule 141.1.b.3
**141.1.b.3.** Units can be affected by spells and game effects that target [[#unit|Units ]]in the [[#trashes|Trash. ]]

#### rule 141.2
**141.2.** A Card Type 

#### rule 141.2.a
**141.2.a.** This is a unique identiﬁer that some spells or abilities will use to restrict what they can choose or affect. 

#### rule 141.2.b
**141.2.b.** The card type is relevant in all zones. 

### rule 142
**142.** [[#damage|Damage ]]is a marked value that is applied to [[#unit|Units. ]]

#### rule 142.1
**142.1.** [[#damage|Damage ]]is not a [[#game object|Game Object. ]]

#### rule 142.2
**142.2.** [[#damage|Damage ]]is a value tracked per-Unit. 

#### rule 142.3
**142.3.** [[#damage|Damage ]]tracks how close a [[#unit|Unit ]]is to being [[#killed|Killed.  ]]See [[##rule 428|rule 428.]] [[#killed|Kill]] for more information. 

#### rule 142.4
**142.4.** [[#damage|Damage ]]can be [[#healed|Healed.  ]]See [[##rule 418|rule 418.]] [[#healed|Heal]] for more information. 

### rule 143
**143.** [[#unit|Units ]]have multiple [[#intrinsic properties|Intrinsic Properties ]]unique to them: 

#### rule 143.1
**143.1.** [[#tags|Tag: ]]A [[#unit|Unit ]]has zero or more [[#tags|Tags ]]representing one or more champions, regions, factions, or species it belongs to. 

#### rule 143.1.a
**143.1.a.** These have no intrinsic rules or behaviors by themselves. 

#### rule 143.1.b
**143.1.b.** Spells, abilities, and game actions can reference these types as part of their execution. 

#### rule 143.2
**143.2.** [[#might|Might]]: The combat statistic of a [[#unit|Unit]]. Used to determine a [[#unit|Unit's ]]contribution to [[#combat|Combat]], as well as when it is [[#killed|Killed ]]by damaging effects. 

#### rule 143.2.a
**143.2.a.** If a [[#unit|Unit ]]ever has nonzero damage marked on it equalling or exceeding its [[#might|Might]], it is [[#killed|Killed. ]]

#### rule 143.2.b
**143.2.b.** If a unit's Might is ever less than 0, it is treated as 0 when referenced by spells and abilities, and when summing Might to be assigned as damage in the [[#combat damage step|Combat Damage Step]]. See [[##rule 460|rule 460.]] [[#combat damage step|The Combat Damage Step]] for more information. 

#### rule 143.2.b.1
**143.2.b.1.** Although the unit’s Might is treated as 0, it is not 0. Effects that calculate Might increases and decreases use the actual value of the unit’s Might. 

#### rule 143.3
**143.3.** [[#unit|Units ]]can have damage marked on them. 

#### rule 143.3.a
**143.3.a.** When spells, abilities, or other game effects deal damage, [[#unit|Units ]]mark that damage on them temporarily. This can be tracked with coins, dice, or other markers, or by memory. 

#### rule 143.3.b
**143.3.b.** [[#damage|Damage ]]is [[#healed|Healed ]]from [[#unit|Units ]]at two speciﬁc times: 

#### rule 143.3.b.1
**143.3.b.1.** At the end of each player's turn. 

#### rule 143.3.b.2
**143.3.b.2.** During a [[#combat cleanup|Combat Cleanup. ]]See [[##rule 461.1|rule 461.1.]]for more information about [[#combat cleanup|Combat Cleanups. ]]

#### rule 143.4
**143.4.** [[#unit|Units ]]enter [[#board exhausted|the Board exhausted. ]]

#### rule 143.4.a
**143.4.a.** This can be altered by [[#accelerate|Accelerate ]]or similar game effects.  See [[##rule 805|rule 805.]] [[#accelerate|Accelerate]] for more information. 

### rule 144
**144.** [[#unit|Units ]]have the [[#inherent ability|Inherent Ability ]]to perform a [[#standard move|Standard Move. ]]

#### rule 144.1
**144.1.** This action is limited in when it can be performed. 

#### rule 144.1.a
**144.1.a.** This action can be done any time during a player's [[#main phase|Main Phase. ]]

#### rule 144.1.b
**144.1.b.** This action cannot be performed during a [[#closed state|Closed State]]. 

#### rule 144.1.c
**144.1.c.** This action cannot be performed during a [[#showdown|Showdown ]]or [[#combat|Combat. ]]

#### rule 144.2
**144.2.** [[#exhausted|Exhausting ]]the [[#unit|Unit ]]is the [[#cost|Cost ]]for this action. 

#### rule 144.3
**144.3.** Players may perform multiple [[#unit|Units' ]]standard move simultaneously. 

#### rule 144.3.a
**144.3.a.** When a [[#move|Move ]]like this is declared by a player, the units' [[#destination|Destination ]]must be the same. 

#### rule 144.3.b
**144.3.b.** When a [[#move|Move ]]like this is declared by a player, the [[#origins|Origins ]]do not need to be the same. 

#### rule 144.3.c
**144.3.c.** The [[#cost|Costs ]]of [[#exhausted|Exhausting ]]the [[#unit|Units ]]are also paid [[#simultaneously|Simultaneously. ]]

#### rule 144.4
**144.4.** The Destinations where [[#unit|Units ]]can [[#move|Move ]]to with their [[#standard move|Standard Move ]]are restricted: 

#### rule 144.4.a
**144.4.a.** [[#unit|Units ]]may move from their [[#bases|Base ]]to a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld. ]]

#### rule 144.4.a.1
**144.4.a.1.** [[#units cannot move|Units cannot Move ]]to a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]that already has units from 2 other players present, or where a [[#combat|Combat ]]is ongoing that has 2 other players as participants. 

#### rule 144.4.b
**144.4.b.** [[#unit|Units ]]may move from a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]to their [[#bases|Base. ]]

#### rule 144.4.c
**144.4.c.** [[#ganking|Ganking ]]is a unique ability that affects a [[#unit|Unit's ]][[#standard move|Standard Move]]

#### rule 144.4.c.1
**144.4.c.1.** [[#unit|Units ]]with [[#ganking|Ganking ]]may use their [[#standard move|Standard Move ]]to [[#move|Move ]]from [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]to [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld.  ]]See [[##rule 810|rule 810.]] [[#ganking|Ganking]] for more information. 

### rule 145
**145.** [[#unit|Units ]]may have [[#activated abilities|Activated Abilities. ]]

#### rule 145.1
**145.1.** [[#activated abilities|Activated Abilities ]]are [[#game effects|Game Effects ]]that are written as [[#cost|Costs ]]followed by a ":", and then succeeded by an effect.  See [[##rule 376|rule 376.]] [[#activated abilities|Activated Abilities]] for more information. 

#### rule 145.2
**145.2.** The [[#activated abilities|Activated Ability ]]of [[#unit|Units ]]may be executed at any time during the controlling player's [[#main phase|Main Phase ]]during an [[#open state|Open State]], and not during a [[#showdown|Showdown. ]]

#### rule 145.2.a
**145.2.a.** This follows the same process as playing a card.  See [[##rule 349|rule 349.]] [[#playing cards|Playing Cards]] for more information. 

#### rule 145.2.a.1
**145.2.a.1.** This behaves, once activated, like a spell without an associated card. 

### rule 146
**146.** [[#unit|Units ]]have a [[#location|Location. ]]

#### rule 146.1
**146.1.** A [[#unit’s location|Unit’s Location ]]is the [[#bases|Base ]]or [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]it currently occupies.

### rule 147
**147.** [[#gear|Gear ]]

### rule 148
**148.** [[#gear|Gear ]]are: 

#### rule 148.1
**148.1.** A [[#game object|Game Object ]]

#### rule 148.1.a
**148.1.a.** While on [[#board|the Board. ]]

#### rule 148.1.a.1
**148.1.a.1.** [[#gear|Gear ]]can only be played to a player's [[#bases|Base ]]unless an effect speciﬁes otherwise. 

#### rule 148.1.a.2
**148.1.a.2.** [[#gear|Gear ]]and their details are Public Information while on [[#board|the Board. ]]

#### rule 148.1.a.3
**148.1.a.3.** [[#gear|Gear ]]can be chosen, affected, or manipulated by spells, effects, or game actions that specify [[#gear|Gear. ]]

#### rule 148.1.a.4
**148.1.a.4.** [[#gear|Gear ]]can be [[#killed|Killed. ]]See [[##rule 428|rule 428.]] [[#killed|Kill]] for more information. 

#### rule 148.1.b
**148.1.b.** While in the [[#trashes|Trash ]]

#### rule 148.1.b.1
**148.1.b.1.** [[#gear|Gear ]]are treated as [[#card|Cards ]]before [[#game object|Game Objects]], similar to the [[#hand|Hand. ]]

#### rule 148.1.b.2
**148.1.b.2.** They retain the properties of being [[#gear|Gear]], but are not on [[#board|the Board ]]and thus cannot take actions or be affected by spells, abilities, or game actions that affect [[#gear|Gear ]]on [[#board|the Board. ]]

#### rule 148.1.b.3
**148.1.b.3.** [[#gear|Gear ]]can be affected by spells and game effects that affect [[#gear|Gear ]]in the [[#trashes|Trash. ]]

#### rule 148.2
**148.2.** A Card Type 

#### rule 148.2.a
**148.2.a.** This is a unique identiﬁer that some spells or abilities will use to restrict what they can choose or affect. 

#### rule 148.2.b
**148.2.b.** The card type is relevant in all zones. 

### rule 149
**149.** [[#gear|Gear ]]have several [[#intrinsic properties|Intrinsic Properties ]]unique to them. 

#### rule 149.1
**149.1.** [[#gear|Gear ]]enter play [[#ready|Ready. ]]

#### rule 149.2
**149.2.** [[#gear|Gear ]]can only be played to a player's [[#bases|Base ]]unless an effect speciﬁes otherwise. 

#### rule 149.3
**149.3.** If an unattached [[#gear|Gear ]]is at a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]for any reason during a cleanup, then it is recalled to its controller's [[#bases|Base ]]as a corrective action.  See [[##rule 449|rule 449.]] [[#recalls|Recalls]] for more information. See [[##rule 318|rule 318.]] [[#cleanup|Cleanups]] for more information. 

### rule 150
**150.** [[#gear|Gear ]]may have [[#activated abilities|Activated Abilities. ]]

#### rule 150.1
**150.1.** [[#activated abilities|Activated Abilities ]]are [[#game effects|Game Effects ]]that are written as [[#cost|Costs ]]followed by a ":", and then succeeded by an effect.  See [[##rule 376|rule 376.]] [[#activated abilities|Activated Abilities]] for more information. 

#### rule 150.2
**150.2.** The [[#activated abilities|Activated Ability ]]of [[#gear|Gear ]]may be executed at any time during the controlling player's [[#main phase|Main Phase ]]during an [[#open state|Open State]], and not during a [[#showdown|Showdown. ]]

#### rule 150.2.a
**150.2.a.** This follows the same process as playing a card. See [[##rule 349|rule 349.]] [[#playing cards|Playing Cards]] for more information. 

#### rule 150.2.a.1
**150.2.a.1.** This behaves, once activated, like a spell without an associated card. 

### rule 151
**151.** [[#gear|Gear ]]have a [[#location|Location. ]]

#### rule 151.1
**151.1.** A [[#gear’s location|Gear’s Location ]]is the [[#bases|Base ]]or [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]it currently occupies. 

#### rule 151.2
**151.2.** [[#gear|Gear ]]cannot normally become located at a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]unless by some special means. Example: Gear are always played to Base. The only exception is a gear played from Facedown, which is played to the Battleﬁeld it was played from. Gear can also become located at a Battleﬁeld if they are attached to a unit who becomes located at a Battleﬁeld. See [[##rule 811|rule 811.]] [[#hide|Hidden]] for more information. See [[##rule 716|rule 716.]] [[#attachment|Attachment]] for more information. 

### rule 152
**152.** [[#spells|Spells ]]

### rule 153
**153.** Spell is a card type. 

### rule 154
**154.** A spell can be played during an [[#open state|Open State ]]outside of [[#showdown|Showdowns ]]on its controller's turn. 

### rule 155
**155.** A spell is controlled by the player who played it. 

### rule 156
**156.** A spell creates a game effect according to its instructions and is then placed in the [[#trashes|Trash ]]of the player who owns it. 

### rule 157
**157.** When a spell is successfully played, a player executes the rules text of the spell. This is called [[#resolving|Resolving ]]the spell. 

#### rule 157.1
**157.1.** Spells have their rules text executed from top to bottom when they are [[#resolving|Resolved. ]]

#### rule 157.2
**157.2.** If a later part of a spell applies a [[#replacement effect|Replacement Effect ]]that alters earlier parts of the spell, apply those replacement effects as appropriate. Example: A spell says "Choose a unit. Kill it the next time it takes damage this turn." and "[Legion] — Kill it now instead. (Get the effect if you've played another card this turn.)" If the Legion condition is satisﬁed, the unit is killed immediately and the instruction to kill it the next time it takes damage is ignored, even if the unit remains on the board somehow. See [[##rule 367|rule 367.]] [[#replacement effect|Replacement Effects]] for more information. 

#### rule 157.3
**157.3.** While a spell or ability on the chain is [[#resolving|Resolving]], no other spells or abilities can be ﬁnalized on the chain or resolved, including triggered abilities or game effects that would occur as a result of the execution of the spell. 

#### rule 157.3.a
**157.3.a.** Finish resolving all effects of a spell before addressing any chain items or Tasks the spell may have added or made outstanding through execution. 

### rule 158
**158.** Certain [[#keywords|Keywords ]]on spells are not executable rules text, but instead intrinsic properties of the spell. 

#### rule 158.1
**158.1.** These determine inherent properties and behaviors of the spell before being played or while on the chain. 

#### rule 158.2
**158.2.** These keywords are: 

#### rule 158.2.a
**158.2.a.** [[#action|Action ]]

#### rule 158.2.a.1
**158.2.a.1.** This indicates that, in addition to being able to be played during an [[#open state|Open State]], this spell may also be played during [[#open state|Open States ]]during [[#showdown|Showdowns. ]]See [[##rule 806|rule 806.]] [[#action|Action]] for more information. 

#### rule 158.2.b
**158.2.b.** [[#reaction|Reaction ]]

#### rule 158.2.b.1
**158.2.b.1.** Grants all cases and rules of [[#action|Action. ]]

#### rule 158.2.b.2
**158.2.b.2.** In addition to all prior cases, may also be played during [[#all forms of closed state|all forms of Closed State. ]]

#### rule 158.2.b.3
**158.2.b.3.** This will result in this spell resolving before spells and abilities that are already on the chain. See [[##rule 813|rule 813.]] [[#reaction|Reaction]] for more information. 

### rule 159
**159.** [[#rune|Runes ]]

### rule 160
**160.** [[#rune|Rune ]]is a [[#card|Card Type. ]]

#### rule 160.1
**160.1.** A [[#rune|Rune ]]is not a [[#main deck|Main Deck ]]card. 

#### rule 160.1.a
**160.1.a.** This means, despite remaining on [[#board|the Board ]]until [[#recycled|Recycled ]]or otherwise removed from the board, it is not a [[#permanents|Permanent. ]]

#### rule 160.2
**160.2.** [[#rune|Runes ]]are kept in the [[#rune deck|Rune Deck. ]]

#### rule 160.2.a
**160.2.a.** Exactly 12 [[#rune|Rune ]]cards chosen during Deck Construction.  See [[##rule 103.3|rule 103.3.]] [[#rune deck|Rune Deck]] for more information. 

#### rule 160.2.b
**160.2.b.** When a [[#rune|Rune ]]is [[#recycled|Recycled ]]it is returned to the [[#rune deck|Rune Deck]], not the [[#main deck|Main Deck.  ]]See [[##rule 416|rule 416.]] [[#recycled|Recycle]] for more information. 

### rule 161
**161.** [[#rune|Runes ]]produce the resources needed to pay costs. 

### rule 162
**162.** [[#rune|Runes ]]produce [[#energy|Energy ]]and [[#power|Power. ]]

#### rule 162.1
**162.1.** [[#energy|Energy ]]is used to pay numeric [[#energy|Energy costs. ]]

#### rule 162.1.a
**162.1.a.** [[#energy|Energy ]]has no Domain. 

#### rule 162.1.b
**162.1.b.** [[#energy|Energy ]]has no type. 

#### rule 162.2
**162.2.** [[#power|Power ]]is used to pay Domain-associated [[#power|Power Costs. ]]

#### rule 162.2.a
**162.2.a.** [[#power|Power ]]has a Domain. 

#### rule 162.2.a.1
**162.2.a.1.** [[#power|Power]]'s Domain usually corresponds to the Domain of the [[#rune|Rune ]]that produced it. 

#### rule 162.2.b
**162.2.b.** Some [[#power|Power ]]is [[#unit|Universal ]]and can be used to pay for costs of any Domain. 

### rule 163
**163.** [[#basic runes|Basic Runes ]]

#### rule 163.1
**163.1.** There are six [[#basic runes|Basic Runes]], each with a Domain corresponding to its name:  Fury Rune  Calm Rune  Mind Rune  Body Rune  Chaos Rune  Order Rune 

#### rule 163.2
**163.2.** A [[#basic runes|Basic Rune ]]always has the following two [[#abilities|Abilities]]: 

#### rule 163.2.a
**163.2.a.** [E]: [Reaction] — Add [1]. 

#### rule 163.2.b
**163.2.b.** Recycle this: [Reaction] — Add [C]. 

#### rule 163.2.b.1
**163.2.b.1.** The [[#power|Power ]]added this way corresponds to the [[#domain|Domain ]]of the [[#rune|Rune ]]that is being [[#recycled|Recycled. ]]

### rule 164
**164.** Rune Pools 

### rule 165
**165.** The [[#rune pool|Rune Pool ]]is a conceptual collection of a player's available [[#energy|Energy ]]and [[#power|Power ]]available to pay [[#cost|Costs. ]]

#### rule 165.1
**165.1.** When a card adds [[#energy|Energy ]]or [[#power|Power, ]]it is added to the controlling player's [[#rune pool|Rune Pool]]. 

#### rule 165.2
**165.2.** Players must ﬁrst add [[#energy|Energy ]]and [[#power|Power ]]to their [[#rune pool|Rune Pool ]]in order to be able to spend it to play cards or pay for [[#abilities|Abilities ]]with costs. 

#### rule 165.3
**165.3.** [[#energy|Energy ]]and [[#power|Power ]]do not have a physical marker or tracker, although players may wish to use a physical tracker if they are retaining unspent [[#energy|Energy ]]and [[#power|Power ]]over the course of their turn. 

### rule 166
**166.** Every player's [[#rune pool|Rune Pool ]]empties at the end of each player's draw phase and the end of each player's turn. 

#### rule 166.1
**166.1.** Any unspent [[#energy|Energy ]]or [[#power|Power ]]are lost. 

### rule 167
**167.** All [[#abilities|Abilities ]]that include the action "[[#added|Add]]" are abilities that are adding [[#energy|Energy ]]or [[#power|Power ]]to the [[#rune pool|Rune Pool. ]]See [[##rule 429|rule 429.]] [[#added|Add]] for more information. 

### rule 168
**168.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]

### rule 169
**169.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]are [[#game object|Game Objects. ]]

#### rule 169.1
**169.1.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]are [[#ownership|Owned ]]by a player. 

#### rule 169.2
**169.2.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]are not shuffled into Decks at the start of a game. 

#### rule 169.2.a
**169.2.a.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]are not played during the course of regular play. 

#### rule 169.2.b
**169.2.b.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]are established at the start of a game and remain in place for the duration of regular play. 

#### rule 169.3
**169.3.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]cannot be [[#killed|Killed ]]during the course of regular play. 

#### rule 169.4
**169.4.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]cannot be [[#move|Moved. ]]

#### rule 169.5
**169.5.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]are [[#location|Locations. ]]

#### rule 169.5.a
**169.5.a.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]can be [[#origins|Origins ]]of moves. 

#### rule 169.5.b
**169.5.b.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]can be [[#destination|Destinations ]]of moves. 

#### rule 169.6
**169.6.** Any number of [[#unit|Units ]]can be present at a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld. ]]

#### rule 169.7
**169.7.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]can be targeted by spells or game effects. 

#### rule 169.8
**169.8.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]can have [[#passive abilities|Passive Abilities. ]]See [[##rule 363|rule 363.]] [[#passive abilities|Passive Abilities]] for more information. 

#### rule 169.9
**169.9.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]can have [[#triggered abilities|Triggered Abilities. ]]See [[##rule 382|rule 382.]] [[#triggered abilities|Triggered Abilities]] for more information. 

#### rule 169.10
**169.10.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]can be referenced in different states in card text: 

#### rule 169.10.a
**169.10.a.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]can be “occupied.” This means they have a [[#unit|Unit ]]present. 

#### rule 169.10.b
**169.10.b.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]can be “uncontrolled.” This means no player controls them. 

#### rule 169.10.c
**169.10.c.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]can be “open.” This means they are unoccupied and uncontrolled. 

### rule 170
**170.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]are not [[#permanents|Permanents. ]]

### rule 171
**171.** The number of [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]on [[#board|the Board ]]is determined by the [[#mode of play|Mode of Play. ]]

### rule 172
**172.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]

### rule 173
**173.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]are [[#game object|Game Objects. ]]

#### rule 173.1
**173.1.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]are [[#ownership|Owned ]]by a player. 

#### rule 173.2
**173.2.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]are not shuffled into Decks at the start of a game. 

#### rule 173.2.a
**173.2.a.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]are not played during the course of regular play. 

#### rule 173.2.b
**173.2.b.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]are established at the start of a game, and remain in place for the duration of regular play. 

#### rule 173.3
**173.3.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]cannot be [[#killed|Killed ]]during the course of regular play. 

#### rule 173.4
**173.4.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]cannot be [[#move|Moved. ]]

#### rule 173.5
**173.5.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]can be targeted by spells or game effects. 

#### rule 173.6
**173.6.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]can have [[#passive abilities|Passive Abilities. ]]See [[##rule 363|rule 363.]] [[#passive abilities|Passive Abilities]] for more information. 

#### rule 173.7
**173.7.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]can have [[#triggered abilities|Triggered Abilities. ]]See [[##rule 382|rule 382.]] [[#triggered abilities|Triggered Abilities]] for more information. 

#### rule 173.8
**173.8.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]can have [[#activated abilities|Activated Abilities. ]]See [[##rule 376|rule 376.]] [[#activated abilities|Activated Abilities]] for more information. 

### rule 174
**174.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]are not [[#permanents|Permanents. ]]

### rule 175
**175.** [[#legend zone|Legends ]]may have one or more [[#domain|Domains. ]]

#### rule 175.1
**175.1.** The [[#legend zone|Legend ]]determines the [[#domain identity|Domain Identity ]]of cards its owner can include. See [[##rule 101|rule 101.]] [[#deck construction|Deck Construction]] for more information. 

### rule 176
**176.** [[#token|Tokens ]]

### rule 177
**177.** [[#token|Tokens ]]are [[#game object|Game Objects ]]created by spells and abilities during play. 

### rule 178
**178.** Tokens can be represented by anything. Printed tokens are included in [[#riftbound|Riftbound ]]booster packs, but they are not required to play a token. 

### rule 179
**179.** A token's [[#control|controller ]]is the controller of the spell or ability that created it, unless the token's type innately determines control or that spell or ability speciﬁes that a different player is the token's controller. 

### rule 180
**180.** A token's [[#ownership|owner ]]is the player who controlled the effect that created it. 

### rule 181
**181.** The effect that creates a token may specify the conditions or circumstances under which it enters the board. These stipulations may alter the usual steps for playing a card. 

#### rule 181.1
**181.1.** The effect may state that the token enters ready or exhausted, if that state is contrary to the default for the token's type. 

#### rule 181.2
**181.2.** The effect may restrict the location to which the token may be played. 

#### rule 181.3
**181.3.** The effect may grant temporary abilities or modiﬁcations to the token. 

### rule 182
**182.** Tokens are not cards. 

#### rule 182.1
**182.1.** Tokens have some properties in common with cards. 

#### rule 182.1.a
**182.1.a.** Tokens are [[#played|played ]]by their owner if their card type is played, following all the applicable steps for playing a card plus any restrictions or modiﬁcations from the effect that created the token.  See [[##rule 349|rule 349.]] [[#playing cards|Playing Cards]] for more information. 

#### rule 182.1.b
**182.1.b.** Token units have a [[#might|Might]]. 

#### rule 182.1.c
**182.1.c.** Tokens may have one or more [[#tags|tags]]. 

#### rule 182.1.d
**182.1.d.** Tokens have a [[#type|type]]. They follow all rules for their type unless otherwise speciﬁed. Example: A token unit is a unit. It enters exhausted, can take the standard move action, deals damage equal to its Might in combat, is destroyed if it takes damage equal to or greater than its might, can be chosen or otherwise affected by spells or abilities that choose or affect units, etc. 

#### rule 182.1.e
**182.1.e.** Tokens inherit the recycle destination of their type. Example: Token runes will be recycled to the Rune Deck. Token units, gear, and spells will be recycled to the Main Deck. Token battleﬁelds and legends can’t be recycled. 

#### rule 182.2
**182.2.** Tokens differ from cards in some ways. 

#### rule 182.2.a
**182.2.a.** Tokens do not have [[#cost|costs]]. 

#### rule 182.2.a.1
**182.2.a.1.** Although tokens do not have costs, their cost is treated as being 0 for all purposes.  

#### rule 182.2.b
**182.2.b.** Tokens do not have [[#domain|domains]]. 

### rule 183
**183.** Tokens are [[#created|Created ]]on the board or the Chain and cannot exist elsewhere. 

#### rule 183.1
**183.1.** If a token is put into any [[#non-board zones|Non-Board Zone ]]besides the chain, it ceases to exist immediately after moving to its new zone. 

### rule 184
**184.** The spell or ability that [[#creates|Creates ]]a token speciﬁes some of its characteristics. It may have other characteristics, as listed below. 

#### rule 184.1
**184.1.** A [[#recruit token|1 [M] Recruit token ]]is a domainless unit token with 1 Might and the Recruit tag. 

#### rule 184.2
**184.2.** A [[#sprite token with temporary|3 [M] Sprite token with Temporary ]]is a domainless unit token with 3 Might, the Fae tag, and the [[#temporary|Temporary ]]keyword. See [[##rule 816|rule 816.]] [[#temporary|Temporary]] for more information. 

#### rule 184.3
**184.3.** A [[#sand soldier token|2 [M] Sand Soldier token ]]is a domainless unit token with 2 Might and the Shurima tag. 

#### rule 184.4
**184.4.** A [[#mech token|3 [M] Mech token ]]is a domainless unit token with 3 Might and the Mech tag. 

#### rule 184.5
**184.5.** A [[#gold gear token|Gold gear token ]]is a domainless gear token with “[Reaction][>] Kill this, [E]: [Add] [A].”  

#### rule 184.6
**184.6.** A [[#reflection token|0 [M] Reflection token ]]is a domainless unit token with 0 Might. 

#### rule 184.7
**184.7.** A [[#bird token|1 [M] Bird token ]]is a domainless unit token with 1 Might, the Bird tag, and the [[#deflect|Deflect ]]keyword. See [[##rule 809|rule 809.]] [[#deflect|Deflect]] for more information. 

#### rule 184.8
**184.8.** A [[#brush battleﬁeld token|Brush battleﬁeld token ]]is a domainless battleﬁeld token with “Bird, Cat, Dog, Poro, and Ivern units here have +1 [M]” and “When you score here, you may replace this with the battleﬁeld it replaced.” 

#### rule 184.9
**184.9.** The [[#baron pit battleﬁeld token|Baron Pit battleﬁeld token ]]is a domainless battleﬁeld token with “Units can move here from anywhere.” 

### rule 185
**185.** [[#control|Control ]]

### rule 186
**186.** [[#control|Control ]]is the concept of a player having influence of a [[#game object|Game Object ]]and applies differently to different card types. 

### rule 187
**187.** [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]

#### rule 187.1
**187.1.** [[#control|Control ]]is established over [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]through the course of play. 

#### rule 187.2
**187.2.** [[#control|Control ]]is a binary state for [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁelds ]]and an [[#identiﬁer|Identiﬁer ]]for players. 

#### rule 187.2.a
**187.2.a.** A [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]is [[#control|Controlled ]]or [[#uncontrolled|Uncontrolled. ]]

#### rule 187.2.b
**187.2.b.** A [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]is [[#controlled by a speciﬁc player|Controlled by a speciﬁc player ]]or [[#controlled by no one|Controlled by no one. ]]

#### rule 187.3
**187.3.** [[#control|Control ]]can be [[#contested|Contested ]]through the course of play. 

#### rule 187.3.a
**187.3.a.** [[#contested|Contested ]]is a temporary status applied to the battleﬁeld when a [[#unit|Unit ]]controlled by a [[#player|Player ]]who does not currently [[#control|Control ]]that [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld Moves ]]or otherwise becomes present there. 

#### rule 187.3.a.1
**187.3.a.1.** [[#unit|Units ]]moving to or being played to a battleﬁeld apply Contested status if that battleﬁeld is not already contested and that [[#unit|Unit]]’s controller does not already control that battleﬁeld. 

#### rule 187.3.b
**187.3.b.** A [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]remains [[#contested|Contested ]]until [[#control|Control ]]is established or re-established. 

#### rule 187.3.c
**187.3.c.** The state of a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]being [[#contested|Contested ]]is used to determine when [[#combat|Combat ]]should occur, when a [[#non-combat showdown|Non-Combat Showdown ]]should occur, and when [[#control|Control ]]will change. 

#### rule 187.3.d
**187.3.d.** At this time [[#game effects|Game Effects ]]cannot reference this status. 

#### rule 187.4
**187.4.** [[#control|Control ]]is established by having [[#unit|Units ]]at a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]at the end of a Showdown or Combat after applying the contested status. 

#### rule 187.4.a
**187.4.a.** If a player controls [[#unit|Units ]]at a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld, ]]outside of [[#combat|Combat, ]]they maintain [[#control|Control ]]of that [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]for as long as they have [[#unit|Units ]]at that [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld. ]]

#### rule 187.4.b
**187.4.b.** While a [[#combat|Combat ]]or [[#showdown|Showdown ]]is ongoing at a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld]], [[#control|Control ]]of that [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]cannot change until instructed by steps of the [[#combat|Combat ]]or [[#showdown|Showdown]]. 

#### rule 187.4.c
**187.4.c.** If a player has no [[#unit|Units ]]at a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]and the turn is in an [[#open state|Open ]]state, they lose [[#control|Control ]]of that [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]in the following cleanup, unless there is a [[#combat|Combat ]]or [[#showdown|Showdown ]]ongoing there. 

#### rule 187.5
**187.5.** [[#control|Control ]]is a constant state. 

#### rule 187.6
**187.6.** [[#control|Control ]]of a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]determines [[#control|Control ]]of its [[#abilities|Abilities. ]]

#### rule 187.6.a
**187.6.a.** While a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]is [[#control|Controlled]], its [[#control|Controller ]]controls its [[#abilities|Abilities]]. That player takes responsibility for adding them to the [[#chain|Chain ]]if applicable, and makes all choices required by them unless otherwise speciﬁed. 

#### rule 187.6.b
**187.6.b.** While a [[#battleﬁelds|Battleﬁeld ]]is [[#uncontrolled|Uncontrolled]], its [[#abilities|Abilities ]]are also [[#uncontrolled|Uncontrolled. ]]The [[#turn player|Turn Player ]]takes responsibility for adding them to the [[#chain|Chain ]]if applicable, makes all choices required by them unless otherwise speciﬁed, and is treated as their [[#control|Controller ]]if any game rule or effect requires one. Example: The Arena’s Greatest is a battleﬁeld that reads “At the start of each player's ﬁrst Beginning Phase, that player gains 1 point.” This ability will usually trigger while the battleﬁeld has no controller. If it does, the Turn Player goes through the steps of adding the ability to the chain and receives priority after doing so, exactly as if they controlled the ability. 

#### rule 187.6.c
**187.6.c.** “You” in a battleﬁeld’s abilities refers to the battleﬁeld’s [[#control|Controller]], as does the implied “you” in instructions like “draw 1.” If the battleﬁeld has no [[#control|Controller]], “you” refers to no one, and all such instructions are ignored. 

### rule 188
**188.** [[#everything else|Everything Else ]]

#### rule 188.1
**188.1.** When a player [[#play|Plays ]]a [[#card|Card ]]or other [[#game object|Game Object]], they are established as that [[#game object|Game Object's ]][[#control|Controller.]]

#### rule 188.2
**188.2.** For [[#spells|Spells]], they are the [[#spells|Spell's ]][[#control|Controller.]]

#### rule 188.2.a
**188.2.a.** That player chooses targets. 

#### rule 188.2.b
**188.2.b.** That player chooses modes. 

#### rule 188.2.c
**188.2.c.** That player pays costs. 

#### rule 188.3
**188.3.** For [[#permanents|Permanents ]]and [[#rune|Runes]], when they [[#enter the board|Enter the Board]], that player is assigned as that [[#game object|Game Object's ]][[#control|Controller.]]

#### rule 188.3.a
**188.3.a.** That player may make decisions about the [[#game object|Game Object's ]][[#inherent ability|Inherent Abilities.]]

#### rule 188.3.b
**188.3.b.** That player may make decisions about the [[#game object|Game Object's ]][[#unique abilities|Unique Abilities.]]

#### rule 188.3.c
**188.3.c.** That player may make decisions about any game effects or decisions necessary while the card is being played. 

#### rule 188.3.d
**188.3.d.** That player may make decisions about any game effects created from "When you play me" effects of [[#permanents|Permanents. ]]

#### rule 188.4
**188.4.** For [[#abilities|Abilities]], they are the [[#ability’s controller|Ability’s Controller. ]]

#### rule 188.4.a
**188.4.a.** By default, the [[#control|Controller ]]of an [[#ability’s source|Ability’s Source ]]is the [[#control|Controller ]]of that [[#abilities|Ability. ]]

#### rule 188.4.b
**188.4.b.** Changes to [[#control|Control ]]of an [[#ability’s source|Ability’s Source ]]do not change [[#control|Control ]]of that [[#abilities|Ability. ]]

#### rule 188.4.c
**188.4.c.** That player chooses targets. 

#### rule 188.4.d
**188.4.d.** That player chooses modes. 

#### rule 188.4.e
**188.4.e.** That player pays costs. 

### rule 189
**189.** When a game effect or rules text refers to the [[#control|Controller ]]of a speciﬁc object, it can be referring to either context interchangeably. 

#### rule 189.1
**189.1.** The method of assignment of control is different, but the status of [[#control|Control ]]is the same across all [[#game object|Game Objects. ]]

## rule 300
**300.** Playing the Game 

### rule 301
**301.** [[#turn order|The Turn ]]

### rule 302
**302.** Play continues cyclically until one player wins. 

### rule 303
**303.** The phases of a turn are rigid, but the actions taken during those steps can be done in any order, unless otherwise speciﬁed. 

#### rule 303.1
**303.1.** [[#game actions|Game Actions ]]of any nature are performed one at a time and are executed completely. 

#### rule 303.2
**303.2.** [[#game actions|Game Actions ]]cannot be performed simultaneously for any reason. 

#### rule 303.2.a
**303.2.a.** If one or more game actions, game effects, or [[#triggered abilities|Triggered Abilities ]]are activated simultaneously, then [[#turn order|Turn Order ]]is referenced to organize the sequence of actions.  See [[##rule 382|rule 382.]] [[#triggered abilities|Triggered Abilities]] for more information. 

### rule 304
**304.** The [[#turn player|Turn Player ]]is the player taking the current turn. 

### rule 305
**305.** When there are no items on the [[#chain|Chain ]]and the [[#turn player|Turn Player ]]cannot or chooses not to perform any [[#discretionary actions|Discretionary Actions]], the current phase or step of the turn ends and the next phase, step, or turn begins. 

### rule 306
**306.** The [[#turn player|Turn Player ]]changes when the current [[#turn player|Turn Player ]]reaches the [[#energy|End ]]of all of the [[#phases|Phases ]]of their [[#turn order|Turn. ]]

### rule 307
**307.** States of the Turn 

### rule 308
**308.** At any given time, the turn is in either a [[#neutral state|Neutral State ]]or a [[#showdown|Showdown State. ]]

#### rule 308.1
**308.1.** If a [[#showdown|Showdown ]]or [[#combat|Combat ]]is in progress, the turn is in a [[#showdown|Showdown State. ]]

#### rule 308.1.a
**308.1.a.** Only cards and abilities with the [[#action|Action ]]or [[#reaction|Reaction ]]keywords can be played or activated in a [[#showdown|Showdown State. ]]

#### rule 308.2
**308.2.** If no [[#showdown|Showdown ]]or [[#combat|Combat ]]is in progress, the turn is in a [[#neutral state|Neutral State. ]]

### rule 309
**309.** At any given time, the turn is in either an [[#open state|Open State ]]or a [[#closed state|Closed State. ]]

#### rule 309.1
**309.1.** If a [[#chain|Chain ]]exists, the turn is in a [[#closed state|Closed State. ]]

#### rule 309.1.a
**309.1.a.** Only cards and abilities with the [[#reaction|Reaction ]]keyword can be played or activated in a [[#closed state|Closed State. ]]

#### rule 309.2
**309.2.** If no [[#chain|Chain ]]exists, the turn is in an [[#open state|Open State. ]]

### rule 310
**310.** These descriptions can be combined, such that the turn is always in one of these four states: 

#### rule 310.1
**310.1.** [[#neutral open|Neutral Open: ]]There is no [[#showdown|Showdown ]]or [[#combat|Combat ]]in progress and no [[#chain|Chain ]]exists. 

#### rule 310.1.a
**310.1.a.** By default, cards can be played and abilities activated only when a player has priority on their turn in a [[#neutral open|Neutral Open ]]state. 

#### rule 310.2
**310.2.** [[#neutral closed|Neutral Closed: ]]There is no [[#showdown|Showdown ]]or [[#combat|Combat ]]in progress and a [[#chain|Chain ]]exists. 

#### rule 310.3
**310.3.** [[#showdown|Showdown Open: ]]A [[#showdown|Showdown ]]or [[#combat|Combat ]]is in progress and no [[#chain|Chain ]]exists. 

#### rule 310.4
**310.4.** [[#showdown closed|Showdown Closed: ]]A [[#showdown|Showdown ]]or [[#combat|Combat ]]is in progress and a [[#chain|Chain ]]exists. 

### rule 311
**311.** Priority and Focus 

### rule 312
**312.** At any given time, up to one player has [[#priority|Priority. ]]

#### rule 312.1
**312.1.** [[#priority|Priority ]]is the singular exclusive right to take [[#discretionary actions|Discretionary Actions. ]]See [[##rule 410.1|rule 410.1.]] [[#discretionary actions|Discretionary Actions]] for more information. 

#### rule 312.1.a
**312.1.a.** The player with [[#priority|Priority ]]can take appropriately timed [[#discretionary actions|Discretionary Actions. ]]

#### rule 312.1.b
**312.1.b.** If no player has [[#priority|Priority]], no player can take [[#discretionary actions|Discretionary Actions. ]]

#### rule 312.1.b.1
**312.1.b.1.** Players can always take and make choices for [[#limited actions|Limited Actions ]]when instructed, regardless of [[#priority|Priority. ]]

#### rule 312.2
**312.2.** A player receives [[#priority|Priority ]]at the following times: 

#### rule 312.2.a
**312.2.a.** When the turn is in a [[#neutral open|Neutral Open State ]]during their [[#main phase|Main Phase. ]]

#### rule 312.2.b
**312.2.b.** When the turn is in a [[#showdown|Showdown State ]]and they gain [[#focus|Focus. ]]

#### rule 312.2.c
**312.2.c.** When the turn is in a [[#closed state|Closed State ]]and they control the next item on the [[#chain|Chain. ]]

#### rule 312.2.d
